It is built on standard HTML mechanisms and is hosted together with the communication server, from which it is downloaded automatically at application startup. The communication server is based upon a well-known CouchDB database system and can be integrated with existing database setups, such as SAP, and can be configured separately to include services and to manage user accounts.
